< review>
My experience here on a Saturday afternoon was more pleasant than I expected, given the prior reviews.  There was only one person ahead of me and it only took about five minutes to get me in for vitals, then another ten to do a test/see the doctor.  I came in prepared with all my paperwork and what I thought might be my diagnosis.  I was in a lot of inexplicable pain, and I couldn't wait through the weekend, so that's how I wound up here.  Turns out my problem wasn't what I thought, and the doctor was quick and efficient, helping to rule out anything I considered to be a possible ailment.  I didn't end up with a result--only saying to check up with my Primary Care when I got a chance to be sure everything was okay, and to take tylenol for pain until then.

The office was clean but obviously worn, the floor could use a good wax job, but the two men (RN and Doc) were polite but all business.  I would go here over Mike's Walk-In Clinic.  You can also get a $20 off coupon from their website for walk-ins, which helps out.</review>

<rating>5< /rating><text>I take my tapas seriously and this one is EASILY MY FAVORITE. Guarantee that whatever you order here is going to be phenomenal. Still thinking about my last visit...

Beef Tongue - cooked to perfection. incredibly juicy and tender. HOW

Chicken Thigh - AMEN x100. This is the juiciest chicken I've ever had. So good that we ordered a second plate of this. Needless to say, this was the highlight of our dinner!!!

Kobe Beef Wrapped Uni - this was my first time having raw meat and i thought it was going to be chewy but it was really tender. i really loved the leaf/herb that was wrapped inside.

The pork belly, omelette, & sashimi were also all solid. We ended our meal with a huge mound of gobo chips which were so addicting!!! They taste like thinly sliced potato chips.

The chicken meatball was the only dish I wouldn't get again. I didn't really like the mushy texture and it was marinated which was a bit sweet for me.

My sister and her fiance have been to several izakayas in LA and Japan and they say this is the only place comparable to the one you find overseas. All of us were still raving about how amazing the food was on the car ride back home and the following day. I honestly would make the hour drive to Torrance just for this!!!< /text>< Pics>

I stumbled upon this place on yelp while searching for an izakaya type of restaurant. However, I am adding this spot to one my top favorites Japanese restaurant without a questions after I came here!!

Beef tongue (5/5): One of my favorite dishes of the night, I love the medium rare beef tongue with the salty yuzu sauces.

A Japanese friend of mine took me here. Very authentic, but that is what you get in Torrance CA.  There's a large Asian (Japanese) population and the quality of the restaurants are amazing.  Hachi does not disappoint.  We are at the counter and had a variety of dishes.  I have to say the the hot pot was at the top of the list.  Very well done and mirrors the food you get in Tokyo. <gmapID>0x80dd4abb7598b7c5:0x659863c45b360ee5</gmapID><text>I'm a regular at Izakaya Hachi and I was hesitant to review since this place is already packed and didn't want it to get more packed. However, it seems like the word is out and I'll share my insider tip. Here we go

Tip: Make reservation a week ahead ( yes it is worth the wait) unless you want to be waiting around 9pm and seated around 9:45.

My go to order for 2 to get a taste of everything best:
Gobo Chips
Fried Agedashi Tofu
Seared Beef Outside Skirt
PORK SHABU SHABU for one person (they give you ramen noodles at the end! cook only for 3 minutes! Tip: they charge extra for added broth, so don't let the existing broth evaporate too quickly - once it's boiling bring the temperature down to a nice simmer)
When in season (raw liver)
On top of all this I always order white fish sashimi that's on their daily special menu (about 4 pieces and it is so fresh-melts-in-your-mouth good)

Drink:
Must try Kigen Kawaba beer both Sunrise & Snow Weizen Beer - so fresh and clean

Some other popular ones:
Creamy Crab Croquette
Jidori Chicken Karaage (for my chicken lovers, unfortunately I cannot eat Chicken)
Beef Tongue
Pork Cheek

Tip:
Say "Oishi" for tasty & "Arigato" for thank you.

Enjoy!</text><Rate>5<//Rate></record></dataset><record>

< text>
One of the best izakaya in the area in my opinion. They constantly change their special menu, which normally includes some Japan imported fish for sushi or sashimi. Most of everything there are good, our favorite items are think cut beef tongue, tonkotsu broth shabu, and battera sushi. The battera sushi there is probably one of the best in the greater LA area. Marinated perfectly, slightly sour and mildly sweet, very well balanced. The place is super popular, especially on weekends, reservations are not required but recommended.<//text>

< text>
High Highs and Low Lows

Meaning the good stuff was really good and some of the dishes that I didn't like, I really didn't like, but the highs were so high that it out weighed the lows.

The Ultimate Highs

This is really starting to sound like a pothead review.  I can assure you that you don't need any substance to make this meal amazing though.  Service! We made reservations and when we got there, there was a personalized hand written note greeting us at the table! Even my mom doesn't do that for me! Almost every employee greeted us as we were being seated.  Hospitality at its finest.

Beef Tongue Steak

Like you've never had before, it may sound weird but I assure you the texture and taste will blow your mind.  Who knew I was a fan of tongue?! I guess I should have known since I'm a fan of French Kissing ;)

Beef Sashimi

You heard that right...raw, unseasoned, untouched, premium beef.  The trifecta of beef tongue, rib eye, and beef shoulder.  Don't get fancy with it, eat it with the herbs it comes with on the dish with a little lemon and let it take you on a ride you won't forget.

Tonkatsu Shabu Hot Pot

Freshly sliced pork and a medley of veggies cooked in amazing mouth watering tonkatsu broth with chunks of pork fat all up in it.  Mother of god...it's the freakin' yum!</text>

<Time>1450403173834<//Time>< Review>
I Loveeee Japanese food!!

This place has a little bit of everything. They have shabu shabu, sushi rolls, as well as small plates.

Small plates include beef skirt steak and beef tongue that we ordered. They were all so good! Perfectly cooked and tender, with the right mix of sauce. The gobo chips were pretty addicting too because it has some seaweed pieces on it. The shabu broth was especially good! I've never had a shabu broth that was this tasty before! It's the same broth they use for tonkutsu ramen! And they give you one extra on the side too. Anything after that, they will charge extra.

This is a great place for a date. Request for the back  booths if you want a more intimate seating. :)</Review>

<time>1472094324610<//time><rate>4<//rate>< Review>
Frank's what can I say about this place. If you are local then you know that the staff is laid back. Very laid back. The service to me is fine but to some might rub them the wrong way.

Food from the kitchen never comes out too salty or peppery.  So this is one of the places that I actually use the salt and pepper shaker. Which is totally fine with me.  Others might not like this. I'm OK with it.

Inside has a vintage atmosphere.  Movies have been filmed here.

Coffee is just fine. Lady knows that I only ask for two cups each time I dine. Overall its occasionally a good place to hang out and eat.<//Review>

I love coming here for breakfast. I know their breakfast menu is pretty good. I have no idea about the lunch menu because I've never been there late enough. So, then, about their breakfasts. 4< /Rating>
<text>My Dad and I are both birders, in fact I learned to appreciate birds through him while growing up in east Africa. So, while Dad was visiting, we found time to venture to the Woodbridge Ecological Reserve to view the Sandhill Cranes coming in for the evening. Although the North Site viewing area had no birds, the South Area looked promising. When dusk was just beginning we heard the cranes flying in, a beautiful sound! However, we realized the cranes were landing in an area further south. Once we moved down the road, we saw many cranes. Checking the South Area viewing site on the return, we saw about 5 cranes had eventually landed there. I hope our presence wasn't too disturbing to the cranes.</text>< pictures>

<UserId.>104682806994746944362<//UserId.><review>We arrived just as the first major flight of Sandhill Cranes came in. Hundreds wheeling and gliding in the 20 knot Delta breeze, some even flying in place against the wind.

We heard the characteristic Sandhill squawk from all directions. Kept looking till a magnificent orange and purple sunset ended the show.

Be sure to read up on the web to find when staff are on hand to guide and explain.< /review>< Date>

< Review>
I'm usually never convinced to purchase things at the mall due to the price vs quality I've experienced in the past. However, when the stress of finding a last minute suit for a family event you really don't have much of a choice. My husband and I came here and he found a suit to rent only to confuse the date of the event. We came to the realization far too late and we couldn't change the rent date or get a refund on time, but Moses who understood our predicament, offered my husband a discount on a purchase. We jumped on it and even got our toddler a cute little tux to boot. Moses did a quick alteration to his little tux and was kind enough to cut a piece of my husband's handkerchief to make one for our son as well as throwing in a free bow tie so that he would match Daddy's shirt. Will be coming back again.</Review>
